 The goal of the project included in this program is to ensure that government services are available to citizens through electronic means and that people get the benefit of the latest information and communication technology
 cabinet kii baithak ke baad doorsanchaar mantri ravishankar prasad ne kaha, ‘7 agast, 2014 ko digital india program par pradhanmantri kii baithak ke dauraan kaarykram kii dizin par kiye gaye pramukh nirnyon ke maddenjar yah manjuuri di gai he

 swasthya, shiksha aadi jaisi sarkari sevaayen maang ke anuroop uplabdh karai ja saken or digital madhyam se sakshartaa ke jariye nagarikon ko shashakt banaaya ja sake

 Mehmood was born on September 29, 1932 in Mumbai
 unke pita mumtaj ali bombai tokies studio main kaam karte the

 'padosan' 60 ke dashak kii jabardast hit sabit hui thi
